 DAILY WATER BALANCE

 J=julian day, Y=simulation year
 P= precipitation       
 RM=rainfall+irrigation+snowmelt
 Q=daily runoff over eff length, Ep=plant transpiration
 Es=soil evaporation, Er=residue evaporation
 Dp=deep percolationlatqcc=lateral subsurface flow 
 UpStrmQ=Runon added to OFE
 SubRIn=Subsurface runon added to OFE
 Total Soil Water=Unfrozen water in soil profile
 frozwt=Frozen water in soil profile
 Snow Water=Water in surface snow
 QOFE=daily runoff scaled to single OFE 
 Tile=Tile drainage (mm)
 Irr=Irigation (mm)
 Area=Area that depths apply over (m^2)
